To compute the sum from \( n = 70 \) to \( 75 \) of \( \text{ADJ}[n] \), we first recognize that each term forms a geometric sequence with the first term \( \text{ADJ}[70] \) and a common ratio of 12. 

The sum of this geometric series can be calculated using the formula for the sum of a finite geometric series:

\[
S = a \frac{r^n - 1}{r - 1}
\]

where:
- \( a = \text{ADJ}[70] \)
- \( r = 12 \)
- \( n = 6 \) (since we are summing from \( n = 70 \) to \( n = 75 \), inclusive)

Calculating the sum:

\[
S = \text{ADJ}[70] \times \frac{12^6 - 1}{12 - 1}
\]

First, compute \( 12^6 \):

\[
12^6 = 2985984
\]

Then subtract 1:

\[
2985984 - 1 = 2985983
\]

Next, divide by 11:

\[
\frac{2985983}{11} = 271453
\]

Thus, the sum is:

\[
S = \text{ADJ}[70] \times 271453
\]

Therefore, the final answer is:

\[
\boxed{271453 \cdot \text{ADJ}[70]}
\]
